  46         if ( f.exists())
  47          f.delete();

6192     private static boolean chkFile()
6193     {
6194         File javaFile=new File("LTTest_java.txt");
6195         if (! javaFile.exists())
6196         {
6197             System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to open file LTTest_java.txt - file not exists!");
6198             return false;
6199         }
6200         File cFile=new File("LTTest_c.txt");
6201         if (! cFile.exists())
6202         {
6203                 System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to open file LTTest_c.txt - file not exists!");
6204                 return false;
6205         }
6206         if ( cFile.length()!=javaFile.length() )
6207         {
6208             System.out.println("FAIL:File length not equal!");
6209             return false;
6210         }
6211         long byteCount=cFile.length();
6212         try{
6213             FileInputStream fisC=new FileInputStream(cFile);
6214             FileInputStream fisJava=new FileInputStream(javaFile);
6215             byte[] cData=new byte[fisC.available()];
6216             fisC.read(cData);
6217             byte[] javaData=new byte[fisJava.available()];
6218             fisJava.read(javaData);
6219             for ( int cnt=0;cnt<byteCount;++cnt)
6220             {
6221                 if ( cData[cnt]!=javaData[cnt] )
6222                 {
6223                     System.out.println("FAIL:Test failed! "+cnt+" byte are wrong! C file - " + cData[cnt] + " Java file - "+javaData[cnt] );
6224                     return false;
6225                 }
6226             }
6227         }
6228         catch (FileNotFoundException ex)
6229         {
6230             System.out.println("FAIL:Some of files not found!");
6231             return false;
6232         }
6233         catch (IOException ex)
6234         {
6235             System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to read files!");
6236             return false;
6237         }
6238         System.out.println("PASS: all data passed correctly!");
6239         return true;
6240     }
